  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_8d893bd6-7a9f-490a-9f44-49c734dbc07a'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };

      initAppleId();
    } else {
      initializeSiwa();

<span id="freeTextContainer12007265310391536212">Roxie’s on the run from a bad boyfriend who will not catch the hint that it is o-v-e-r.   <span id="freeText12007265310391536212" style="display:none">Roxie’s on the run from a bad boyfriend who will not catch the hint that it is o-v-e-r. She’s in no mood for love at first sight, but when her eyes fall on Hank, it’s trouble from the get-go. Roxie tries to hold Hank at arms length but Hank wants to be a closer (as in, a lot closer). Roxie’s trouble catches up with her and Hank wants to help but Roxie knows in her heart that she’s no good for a white hat guy. The problem is no one agrees with her, especially her crazy hippie best friend Annette or her parents; the even crazier small-Indiana-town Herb and Trish. Toss into the mix the gang from Rock Chick and Rock Chick Rescue and Roxie finds herself totally outnumbered.<br /><br />Climb in for another Rock Chick wild ride through Rock Chick Redemption. As the odds stack up against Roxie, she has no choice but to hold on and just ride it out through the kidnappings, car chases, society parties, a riot at the strip club, Hank getting “Mom Bombed” and one crazy night at the Haunted House.<br /><br />During all this Hank works at convincing her she really wants to stay and he, along with the Hot Bunch, go all out to make her safe. Hank also needs to work on showing Roxie that her past decisions don’t mean her future can’t include something as downright delicious as… normal.</span>
  <a data-text-id="12007265310391536212" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

    <div class="section firstReview">
      

<div id="review_416700593" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/416700593" />
    <a title="Stacey is Sassy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/12062194-stacey-is-sassy"><img alt="Stacey is Sassy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1474185067p2/12062194.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/416700593?book_show_action=true">Sep 17, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Stacey is Sassy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Stacey is Sassy" href="/user/show/12062194-stacey-is-sassy">Stacey is Sassy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Audible Audio " href="/book/show/22475277-rock-chick-redemption">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12062194-stacey-is-sassy?shelf=kristen-ashley">kristen-ashley</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12062194-stacey-is-sassy?shelf=steamy">steamy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12062194-stacey-is-sassy?shelf=cont-series">cont-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12062194-stacey-is-sassy?shelf=audio">audio</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer416700593" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17710425257412294189"><b>I knew it would happen...</b><br/><br/>Yep, I love Hank again. This time, he was sweet, loving and so patient with Roxie, I have no idea what I was thinking the last time I listened. Loved all the good bits, cried in all the bad bits.<br/><br/>Great to catch up with my Rock Chick family.<br/><br/>...and I saw Luke 😍😍😍😍<br/><br/>***********<br/><br/><b>Time for another trip around the block with the <i>Rock Chicks</i></b><br/><br/>I feel kind of let down with this re-read/listen of Hank and Roxie's story. To be honest, it was Hank that left me dissatisfied. I feel like we </span>
  <span id="freeText17710425257412294189" style="display:none"><b>I knew it would happen...</b><br><br>Yep, I love Hank again. This time, he was sweet, loving and so patient with Roxie, I have no idea what I was thinking the last time I listened. Loved all the good bits, cried in all the bad bits.<br><br>Great to catch up with my Rock Chick family.<br><br>...and I saw Luke 😍😍😍😍<br><br>***********<br><br><b>Time for another trip around the block with the <i>Rock Chicks</i></b><br><br>I feel kind of let down with this re-read/listen of Hank and Roxie's story. To be honest, it was Hank that left me dissatisfied. I feel like we don't really get to know him. He's always off at work fighting bad guys or telling Roxie off. Now, take this with a grain of salt. The last time I read this one, Hank was the light of my life and his dedication and devotion had me swooning.<br><br>Do you know what I think the problem is? I'm having Luke Stark withdrawals. Getting a little glimpse of him, when he's gruff, hot, smart, hot, bossy, hot and funny...and HOT, just makes me want to skip the next block and head straight to <i>Revenge</i>. I may also be willing to head straight to <i>Revenge</i> because I don't want to "see" Luke meet with <i>Renegade</i>.<br><br>Re-reads/listenings of the <i>Rock Chicks</i> is serious work. You have to be with the one you love and, well, Luke will always be my one true <i>Hot Bunch MAN</i>.<br><br>I love the Rock Chicks and there is no way in bloody HELL I'm changing my rating. It was only a slight dissatisfaction with Hank, next time I see him, I'll love him again.<br><br>*************<br><br><b>Another Rock Chick audio devoured.</b><br><br>I laughed, I cried (on the train...avoiding eye contact with fellow passengers) and I loved every minute of it. Is it freaky that my two favourite parts are -<br><br>1. When she is at her worst and needs saving. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[That it's Vance (who saves her) may have something to do with it. He's all hot, intense and thoughtful. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>2. When Hank loses it and yells at her for putting her life in danger. The fact that she stepped in front of danger to protect him and her loved ones made it even more epic in my mind.<br>I think it's the emotions portrayed that made them my favourite parts. <br><br>Even though Roxie feels so bad about herself (at that particular moment), seeing the care and protection she received made me feel tight in my chest. If I was in the same situation, I would want someone looking out for me when I'm at my worst.<br><br>Hank's reaction to screaming at Roxie seemed very real. I loved that someone so "in control" lost it so epically. I know that I'm guilty of screaming at my kids when they risk their health and wellbeing. I want my kids to be happy and safe at all times and I think this was why Hank yelled.<br><br>Hank is the serious one in the group. He seems to watch everything going on around him and observe the proceedings. When it's needed, he says what needs to be said. Sometimes, even he can't control his actions and reactions. I would have loved to be a fly on the wall when he lost it. I'm pretty sure he would be EXTREMELY passionate.<br><br>Roxie's love for fashion and dressing up I can totally relate to. Her need to always present herself in the best light is something I (try to) do as well. I can't remember the last time I left my house without lipstick on and my hair not done.<br><br>Honestly, I do struggle a little with the way the Rock Chicks push away their men...for their man's benefit. Hello...if the hot bunch guy is up for the challenge, go with the flow. <br><br><i>Rock Chick Redemption</i> is about finding the love of your life and finding the person who will put up with you through the good and the bad. No love is perfect and nobody is perfect.<br><br>As per usual...the <i>Rock Chick</i> gang makes <i>Rock Chick Redemption</i> fun and interesting. I want my own <i>Rock Chick</i> gang...and a <i>Hot Bunch</i> too.<br><br>For some reason, the odd numbers in this series are my favourite. (Rubbing my hands together in delight) Luke and Ava are up next.<br><br>To buy <i>Rock Chick Redemption</i> from Amazon - <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://amzn.to/2dhfzDX">http://amzn.to/2dhfzDX</a><br><br><b>I’m an Aussie chick who loves to read and review romance, drink coffee, be a <i>Style Setter</i> and stalk David Gandy. To see more of my reviews, fashion, food and pervathons -</b><br><br><a href="http://staceyissassy.com/" rel="nofollow noopener"> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1447925695i/17069306.jpg" width="170" height="170" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><a href="https://www.facebook.com/Sassyreviews" rel="nofollow noopener"> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1440644070i/16004243.jpg" width="40" height="40" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><a href="https://www.pinterest.com/Stacey1565/" rel="nofollow noopener"> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1440644070i/16004244.jpg" width="40" height="40" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><a href="https://www.twitter.com/StaceyisSassy" rel="nofollow noopener"> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1440644070i/16004245.jpg" width="40" height="40" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:

        <div class="reviewText stacked">

<span id="freeTextContainer17185967089732872203"><b>3.5 “Whisky” STARS</b><br/><br/><span>[image error]</span><br/><br/>In complete contrast to the prior book where I loved hero and didn’t care for heroine, this one is the complete opposite. I truly liked the heroine, Roxie and found the hero, Hank Nightingale drawing similar emotions to Mitch-The Lawman for me. Hank sadly was just okay, meh, in this story. Hey it happens.<br/><br/><b>
  <i>”You were here to see your uncle until you stepped into Fortnum’s and saw me and I saw you. You know it and I kow it. You want me to convince you. I’m prepared </i></b></span>
  <span id="freeText17185967089732872203" style="display:none"><b>3.5 “Whisky” STARS</b><br><br><span>[image error]</span><br><br>In complete contrast to the prior book where I loved hero and didn’t care for heroine, this one is the complete opposite. I truly liked the heroine, Roxie and found the hero, Hank Nightingale drawing similar emotions to Mitch-The Lawman for me. Hank sadly was just okay, meh, in this story. Hey it happens.<br><br><b>
  <i>”You were here to see your uncle until you stepped into Fortnum’s and saw me and I saw you. You know it and I kow it. You want me to convince you. I’m prepared to do that.” Yowza</i>
</b><br><br>Roxie, Tex’s niece is very relatable, funny and didn’t over do her freak outs. Thankfully, she wasn’t hard of hearing (Pardon? Excuse me?) She has her own friends, a great family and killer fashion style. She just has one problem an ex that refuses to be an ex. She has been trapped in a relationship that she has countless times tried to flee. I found the whole Billy the ex's story line interesting and exciting. Roxie’s family was fabulous, she was lovable and overall she made Hank’s story worth the read.<br> <br><b>
  <i>”My life began when I met you”</i>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_692298177" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/692298177" />
    <a title="Christy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11284813-christy"><img alt="Christy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1594293998p2/11284813.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/692298177?book_show_action=true">Aug 11, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christy" href="/user/show/11284813-christy">Christy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer692298177" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15420865908743745463"><b>5 Whisky Stars!</b><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/db7f7d3a-b4cf-43c7-be54-7549771eddc2_zpsf88690f3.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380432702i/869491.jpg' alt=' photo db7f7d3a-b4cf-43c7-be54-7549771eddc2_zpsf88690f3.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><b>
  <blockquote>When you fuck up, you have to admit it, deal with it, and move on.</blockquote>
</b> That is Roxie’s motto. And thats what she’s trying to do. After dealing with a loser boyfriend for the last seven years, Roxie is ready to start over. So she’s going to Denver temporarily to get away. She wants to meet her Uncle Tex, so what better place to go. She goes to Tex’s place of employment and she sees something you just don’t see every day... A plethora of hot men.<br/><b>
  <blockquote>It looked like GQ was having a</blockquote></b></span>
  <span id="freeText15420865908743745463" style="display:none"><b>5 Whisky Stars!</b><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/db7f7d3a-b4cf-43c7-be54-7549771eddc2_zpsf88690f3.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380432702i/869491.jpg" alt=" photo db7f7d3a-b4cf-43c7-be54-7549771eddc2_zpsf88690f3.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>
  <blockquote>When you fuck up, you have to admit it, deal with it, and move on.</blockquote>
</b> That is Roxie’s motto. And thats what she’s trying to do. After dealing with a loser boyfriend for the last seven years, Roxie is ready to start over. So she’s going to Denver temporarily to get away. She wants to meet her Uncle Tex, so what better place to go. She goes to Tex’s place of employment and she sees something you just don’t see every day... A plethora of hot men.<br><b>
  <blockquote>It looked like GQ was having a convention and all the best looking guys had decided to have a coffee at Fortnum's before going to seminars on how to cope with being really, unbelievably, fucking gorgeous.</blockquote>
</b> Among all the hot men, there is one that catches her eye right away. He has whisky colored eyes. Hank Nightingale. Hank is Lee Nightingale’s brother and a police officer. Once he see’s Roxie, he’s done. He knows he’s gotta have her. with all her trouble, Roxie doesn’t think she is good for Hank. Hank knows better. He wants to help Roxie deal with her problems. Once she’s with Hank, she is his wether she wants to be or not. <br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>“I'm protecting what's mine."<br>"I'm not yours," I said. <br>"You're welcome to think that but it doesn't change the fact that you are.”</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/4d9eb41e-10f6-4740-afbc-4f8d220fd998_zps096ec327.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380432702i/869492.jpg" alt=" photo 4d9eb41e-10f6-4740-afbc-4f8d220fd998_zps096ec327.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Poor Roxie goes through the ringer. Between her stalker ex-boyfriend being after her, kidnappings, shoot outs, car chases, there is never a dull moment. Through all this, Roxie just wants to be done with her ex, and get away from all the awesome people she has met in Denver. She doesn’t feel like she’s any good for them with all the trouble she’s brought around. Especially Hank. She could never be good enough for Hank. She tries to end things with him MANY times, but these badass hotties don’t take no for an answer. Hank just has to have a few ‘conversations’ with her and it’s all good. <br><i>
  <blockquote>“You’re not breakin’ up with me,” he said.<br>“I am.” I told him.<br>“You’re not.” <br>“Hank, I am.”<br> “Sunshine, you are not.”<br> “You can’t tell me I’m not breaking up with you when I’m breaking up with you!” <br>“I think I just did.”</blockquote>
</i><br>Hank just has to convince Roxie that she her past mistakes don’t dictate her future. And he wants a future with her. As much as she tries to deny it, there is nothing Roxie would love more than a future with Hank.<br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/4a1380e7-6303-4a1a-b8ea-5403bfaa7a75_zps81ba915f.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380432702i/869493.jpg" alt=" photo 4a1380e7-6303-4a1a-b8ea-5403bfaa7a75_zps81ba915f.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Roxie was the funniest heroine. I just adored her and her high maintenance self. She made me laugh more times than I could count. And she was pretty damn cute. Then there is Hank. I loved what little bit of Hank we got in the first two books, and I love him even more now. His protective nature and sweet, sexy self... Mmmm. <br><br>There were SO many parts of this book I just loved... There were some touching moments: First meet with Uncle Tex, ‘She’s the One’, and Roxie’s speech at the end. I can’t even tell you how many lol funny parts there were but some that are sticking out: The haunted house (OMG I almost peed myself reading about that- it’s so me!), Poor Hank getting mom bombed, and pretty much ANY scene with Roxie’s parents (They were a hoot!). I just loved the Sunshine/Whisky pet names. It made me melt a bit. Hank and Roxie has some hot chemistry. I loved ‘erasing the day’. We also get to really meet another member of Lee’s boys- Luke... Luke... Luke Stark. Need I say more? I think I’m in love with that one! <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/d6506f7d-a60d-4a51-b041-ae1a26da6728_zps6e0147d6.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380432702i/869494.jpg" alt=" photo d6506f7d-a60d-4a51-b041-ae1a26da6728_zps6e0147d6.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Oh these Rock Chick books just get better and better! The first two were good, but this one was just fabulous! Loved Hank, loved Roxie, loved the story! Full of humor, fun, sex, love, suspense and more alpha males than you will know what to do with! I’m serious... I love my husband, but Kristen Ashley makes me want to go to Denver and scoop up one of these guys! A fabulous series I’m looking forward to continuing!!!</span>
  <a data-text-id="15420865908743745463" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer300045117" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer16209989225482682360"><br/><b> Re-read Review - August 23-25, 2013</b><br/><br/>What a great story! I enjoyed it even more during my re-read, picking up on things I'd missed before, intriguing insights into Hank that explain why so many people worship at his altar! Y'all need to move over and make room for me at said altar, too!<br/><br/>Roxie's growin' on me, but still not my favorite Rock Chick. That said, she is Tex's niece so that gets her some big time brownie points! <br/><br/>Aside from a laugh out loud haunted house scene, meeting Roxie's loopy paren</span>
  <span id="freeText16209989225482682360" style="display:none"><br /><b> Re-read Review - August 23-25, 2013</b><br /><br />What a great story! I enjoyed it even more during my re-read, picking up on things I'd missed before, intriguing insights into Hank that explain why so many people worship at his altar! Y'all need to move over and make room for me at said altar, too!<br /><br />Roxie's growin' on me, but still not my favorite Rock Chick. That said, she is Tex's niece so that gets her some big time brownie points! <br /><br />Aside from a laugh out loud haunted house scene, meeting Roxie's loopy parents, and all the hilarity that is Tex, my favorite part of <i>Rock Chick Redemption</i> is the kick-ass segue into the next book, <i>Rock Chick Renegade</i>, Jules and Vance's story! Yummmmm!<br /><br />Bumping this from 4.5 to a full 5 stars!<br /><br /><b>Original Review - </b><br /><br />Every time I read a Kristen Ashley book I think, ‘this is my favorite!’ and then I move on to the next book and end up thinking, ‘this is my favorite!’… and so it goes. What I’ve come to realize is that I’ll really never be able to pick a favorite because each book offers something <i>different </i>than the others, and I find that that’s what makes me love each one of the books the <i>same</i> "much" as the others.<br /><br />And now that I’ve totally confused you, I’ll just say… I love Hank and Roxie, but for me, Tex really stole the show. I love that man and can’t get enough of his “shee-it.” :)<br /><br />-----<br />If you're a Kristen Ashley addict, or just interested in checking her books, be sure to stop by our <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/group/show/66492-kristen-ashley-addict-s-support-group" rel="nofollow noopener">Kristen Ashley Addict's Support Group</a> here on Goodreads! <br /><br />4.5/5</span>

<div id="review_348609197" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/348609197" />
    <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog"><img alt="Aestas Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1353371225p2/5604583.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/348609197?book_show_action=true">Jun 14, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Aestas Book Blog" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog">Aestas Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer348609197" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16025197970201895963">4.5 Stars<br/><br/>Another winner from Kristen Ashley!! You just can’t help but fall in LOVE with those Nightingale boys!!<br/><br/>I’ve been looking forward to Hank’s book since the beginning of this series and I was not dissapointed. I squeed, snorted, snickered and laughed my way through it – a perfect, fun action-romance read!<br/><br/>Hank Nightingale is basically the ultimate swoooony good guy – he’s a gorgeous, loving, straight-arrow, always-in-control cop with insane loyalty to his family and a huge heart. It was fun</span>
  <span id="freeText16025197970201895963" style="display:none">4.5 Stars<br><br>Another winner from Kristen Ashley!! You just can’t help but fall in LOVE with those Nightingale boys!!<br><br>I’ve been looking forward to Hank’s book since the beginning of this series and I was not dissapointed. I squeed, snorted, snickered and laughed my way through it – a perfect, fun action-romance read!<br><br>Hank Nightingale is basically the ultimate swoooony good guy – he’s a gorgeous, loving, straight-arrow, always-in-control cop with insane loyalty to his family and a huge heart. It was fun to see him come undone by this girl who just walked into his life :) <br><br>He meets Roxie when she comes into town to meet her uncle Tex (who we met as a delightful side character – ex-con turned artisan coffee creator – in the first 2 books of the series) who works at the coffee shop-bookstore run by Indy (the heroine from book 1). There, she runs into all the (uber-Alpha) boys from Nightingale Investigations…<br><br><i> <b> “It looked like GQ was having a convention and all the best looking guys had decided to have coffee at Fornum’s before going to seminars on how to cope with being really, unbelievably, fucking gorgeous.” </b></i> <br><br>… but she finds inexplicably drawn to Hank. Its love at first sight for both of them. Problem is, she’s in a bit of trouble trying to ditch her loser criminal ex-boyfriend. Lucky for her, Hanks is a cop and is more than happy to help her out… and take her out to dinner, woo her into his bed, protect her, claim her as his woman and other utterly swoon-worthy things that only a true Alpha can do best :P <br><br><i> “I’m having dinner with Hank but only because he’s persuasive-”<br>“I bet.”<br>“Its just dinner. Nothing more…”<br>“Dinner may be just dinner in Chicago but it ain’t in Denver. These boys don’t fuck around… Indy was livin’ with Lee after ’bout a day. Jet was with Eddie from my count, after less than a week. The way Hank’s lookin’ at you, I’m guessin’ less than 48 hours.” </i><br><br>And of course, it wouldn’t be a proper KA book without its fair share of car chases, kidnapping (s), hostage situations, shootouts, and crazy ex’s, now would it? lol<br><br>I seriously loved Hank! I loved how insanely sweet, thoughtful, caring and perceptive he was. He saw right through the emotional front that Roxie put up and into her heart and wouldn’t give up until she believed in them too. I love how he saw how much her previous relationship made her wary to put her heart out on the line again and he was willing to made every effort to show that he was worth it.<br><br>Roxie was also a great heroine. She had a fun voice and was stubborn and sassy enough to stand up for herself, but soft and lovable enough to be able to have some seriously heart-melting moments with Hank.<br><br>I loved that by this third book, you really feel like you KNOW all these characters personally – you get all their inside jokes and little gestures, and it just totally maximises the fun! I just loved the huge network of characters and all their inter-relations.<br><br><i> “…heard Ally say, “I’m gonna talk to Lee. The minute they find that asshole, I want my turn with him in the holding room.”<br>“Ally,” said Indy. <br>“Sugar, I’m talking to Marcus to-night.” Daisy broke in. “He’s gotta step his shit up. Ain’t gonna be no holding room for Billy fucking Flynn, not if I have anything to say about it.” </i><br><br>The dialogue in this book was awesome – so many laugh out loud moments! Also, we are introduced to new side characters – namely Luke Stark, the seriously HOT member of Nightingale Investigations who until now was recovering from a gunshot wound – I seriously cannot wait until his book! He is h.o.t. !!<br><br>And nobody writes family scenes like Ms. Ashley – I swear in all her books, the families just make me grin like an idiot.<br><br><i> “Son, let me tell you something. Even if you don’t care, pretend you do. Honestly, it’s the best way to go,” Dad, the voice of experience, decided to wade in. “She talks about toss pillows. You don’t care about toss pillows. You don’t even know what toss pillows are. Pretend that toss pillows are your highest priority in life.” </i><br><br>Really, if you just want a fun read full of Alpha males, swoony romance, and lots of action-packed craziness, this is a great series to start.<br><br><i> “This is crazy. You’re crazy. Denver’s crazy. All you boys skipped right over the last century, didn’t you? I think even the last million years. You’re cavemen” </i><br><br>I’m so looking forward to more from this series. I’ve really turned into quite the KA book addict!!<br><br>Here's how I see Hank and Roxie:<br><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380380813i/737812._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>For more of my reviews, visit <a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Aestas Book Blog</a><br><br>And come join the Aestas Book Blog <a href="http://www.facebook.com/pages/Aestas-Book-Blog/332404836826905" rel="nofollow noopener"> Facebook Page</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="16025197970201895963" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText12022292255928038779" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411068060i/11190622._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="321" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I love this series. </i><br><br>Roxie is crazy ol' Tex's niece, and when she rolls into town, chaos isn't too far behind. Lee's brother, Hank 'Whisky' catches her eye and she catches his. Although Roxie tries to resist, as they all do, Hank is determined. Hank claims Roxie and does everything he can to protect her.<br><br><i>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1500696213?book_show_action=true">Jan 08, 2016</a>

      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25894509-jilly?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25894509-jilly?shelf=buddy-read-with-bbbs">buddy-read-with-bbbs</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25894509-jilly?shelf=contemporary-fiction">contemporary-fiction</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1500696213" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14331696025371779368">Based on just the romance between Roxie and Hank, this would have been a one-star story for me. What saved it is all of the side characters, as usual, and the awesomeness that is Roxie's parents.<br/> <br/>Plus Luke. Gimme, gimme, gimme<br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1452331798i/17679458.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Okay, so what's my problem? It was too much. Too fast. Too pushy. Too creepily alpha-y.<br/>See, there is a formula for these books: Boy alpha decides he wants girl, drags her back to his place, holds her captive while she tries to escape him, forces her to accept a relationship</span>
  <span id="freeText14331696025371779368" style="display:none">Based on just the romance between Roxie and Hank, this would have been a one-star story for me. What saved it is all of the side characters, as usual, and the awesomeness that is Roxie's parents.<br> <br>Plus Luke. Gimme, gimme, gimme<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1452331798i/17679458.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Okay, so what's my problem? It was too much. Too fast. Too pushy. Too creepily alpha-y.<br>See, there is a formula for these books: Boy alpha decides he wants girl, drags her back to his place, holds her captive while she tries to escape him, forces her to accept a relationship with him.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1452331798i/17679459.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>That worked out fine in the first book because Indy and Lee had known each other all of their lives and she had been in love with him forever. It was cute that he was being all forceful about the fact that it was time for them to get together. They knew each other better than anyone else, moving fast was fine.<br>Eddie and Jet were a little too fast, but they had a mutual attraction for about a month before things got intense.<br>But, this Hank and Roxie romance? It was just too much. Too much!!<br>He meets her, asks her out on a date for the next night and she says no. He grabs her and kisses her, without her consent. He then tells her that they ARE going on a date and that, as a cop, he will track her down if she tries to escape said date. Then!! Then, he takes her out on a date and refuses to take her home afterwards but informs her that she will be sleeping with him at his house. She says "no" several times, but he forces himself on her. But, all this is okay because she enjoyed the sex and he's hot. Hmmm...... I'm not so sure I like this message. She explicitly told this guy "no" over and over again, but he continued pursuing her, to the point of having non-consensual sex and not allowing her to leave his house after this sex either, all while threatening her if she tried to get away.<br>Let's say for a minute, that she was serious, and meant the words that came out of her mouth. She said "no" to the date, asked to be taken home after being bullied into the date, said "no" to the sex, tried to leave by calling a cab after the sex, and tried to not see him again or have any kind of relationship with him. These are the facts and the words that she used. His choosing to ignore them was the equivalent of date-rape. But, that's okay, because she was attracted to him and enjoyed herself. What if she wasn't? Put these actions on a man whom she wasn't interested in, and you have clear date-rape? But, why? If a woman says "no", is it really up to the man to decide whether he thinks she means it or not? I don't think they should be the ones deciding this. I think "no" means "no" - no matter what. If he doesn't like her answer, too bad. It's not his choice to take away her choices.<br><br>Okay, off my soapbox. I will take the book as a work of fiction and understand that these alpha-guys are just this book series' formula. If I can put that aside, I appreciate the cast of characters and the funny situations they find themselves in.<br><br>But, I'm taking a break to read Dark Lover with Karly and Jess anyway. There's no over-bearing alpha male in that book at all.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1452331798ra/17679460.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="14331696025371779368" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

Mad as a box of frogs (well she is Tex's niece after all) but with an even worse opinion of herself than Jet in book 2!<br /><br />Also, this book introduces my favourite of the hot bunch! Luke!<br /><br />Loved Hank, you could see how he fell hard and quick, and just wanted to help Roxie. And Roxie, she does not fight this just for the sake of fighting.         <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1488176470" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14524627608737000892"><b>Sale Alert</b> Kindle Deal 14May20 <a href='https://www.amazon.com/dp/B004QS9454/ref=s9_acsd_al_bw_c2_x_17_i?pf_rd_m=ATVPDKIKX0DER&pf_rd_s=merchandised-search-2&pf_rd_r=9EBN1ZMD6K3NG8KH1NM6&pf_rd_t=101&pf_rd_p=3d640a6c-45ca-4115-bc35-150a29d39125&pf_rd_i=11552285011' rel='nofollow noopener'>$0.99</a><br/><br/><b>4.5 Whiskey Colored Stars</b><br/><br/>After a slightly disappointing second book in the series we are now back on track because I loved Hank and Roxie’s story.<br/><br/>We are back to cute and adorable pet names – Whiskey and Sunshine (It works)<br/><br/>We are back to alpha dialogue that makes my heart beat faster and my lady parts tingly <br/><blockquote>
  <i>“I’m gonna have to ask you to stop kissing me,” I whispered, and even to myself I didn’t sound very convincing with my request. <br/>He smiled. “I’m not gonn</i></blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText14524627608737000892" style="display:none"><b>Sale Alert</b> Kindle Deal 14May20 <a href="https://www.amazon.com/dp/B004QS9454/ref=s9_acsd_al_bw_c2_x_17_i?pf_rd_m=ATVPDKIKX0DER&amp;pf_rd_s=merchandised-search-2&amp;pf_rd_r=9EBN1ZMD6K3NG8KH1NM6&amp;pf_rd_t=101&amp;pf_rd_p=3d640a6c-45ca-4115-bc35-150a29d39125&amp;pf_rd_i=11552285011" rel="nofollow noopener">$0.99</a><br /><br /><b>4.5 Whiskey Colored Stars</b><br /><br />After a slightly disappointing second book in the series we are now back on track because I loved Hank and Roxie’s story.<br /><br />We are back to cute and adorable pet names – Whiskey and Sunshine (It works)<br /><br />We are back to alpha dialogue that makes my heart beat faster and my lady parts tingly <br /><blockquote>
  <i>“I’m gonna have to ask you to stop kissing me,” I whispered, and even to myself I didn’t sound very convincing with my request. <br />He smiled. “I’m not gonna stop kissing you, but I’ll wait until tomorrow night to do it again.” <br />His hand fisted gently in my hair and his mouth went to my ear. <br />Then he said, “And, as soon as I can, I’m gonna taste more than your lips.”</i>
</blockquote><br />We are back to crazy, cooky and hilarious talk in the book store. I am seriously thinking of packing up and taking a road trip to Denver to look for Fortmun’s. It has three things I love <b>Books, Coffee and Alphas</b> not necessarily in that order.<br /><br /><b>STUN GUNS!!!!</b> – need I say more. I want to go out and get one after reading this series.<br /><br /><b>Roxie is Tex’s niece</b> – As soon as I saw that I knew I was going to love her. She is sometimes just as crazy as Tex but in a slightly different way.<br /><blockquote>
  <i>“And no alligator tail,” I carried on. “Alligators are cute. I’m not a vegetarian, but I don’t eat cute animals. Like lamb. Lambs are cute. We can try the rattlesnake. I think I could eat snake because snakes freak me out.”</i>
</blockquote><br />No eating cute animals….like alligators. And why are they cute you might ask…well because <i>they always look like they are smiling.</i><br /><br />We are back to having so many great side characters that I don’t even know where to begin with who was the best. <b>Tex</b> almost always wins this contest. He is fantastic but I don’t think Duke gets enough credit either…<br /><blockquote>
  <i>”No offense but you’re gonna run him through the mill, I can tell. And no doubt, we’ll all get ground up with him.”<br />I blinked. “I’m only in town for a couple of days,” I said. <br />“I can see it comin’,” Duke retorted. <br />“Hallelujah!” Uncle Tex boomed. “No lag this time. Keep ‘im hoppin’, darlin’ girl, that’s what I say.”</i>
</blockquote><br />That is Tex always up for a little action or a lot as the case may be.<br /><br />Her parents were hilarious. If they are your parents it isn’t funny but when it is someone else’s well you can’t help but laugh at all the embarrassing and inappropriate things they say in front of EVERYONE. <br /><br />But Annette her BFF wins for best new character addition. She is hilarious, loud, slightly inappropriate but you could tell she was someone who once she decides she is your friend it is a life long bond.<br /><blockquote>
  <i>“Yo, bitch!” she answered on the second ring. <br />This was nothing to be alarmed about. This was how Annette answered the phone all the time. <br />“Hey,” I said, quietly. Then I burst into tears. Then I told her my story, all of my story.<br />“Holy fucking Jesus H. Christ,” she said when I was done. <br />“I know.” <br />“He hasn’t called?” <br />“Annette!” I cried. <br />“Billy kidnapped me and beat me up. This is not about Hank!”</i>
</blockquote><br />But your girl always knows what it is really about….that is why they are your girl. I loved Annette’s quirky granola wanderer ways they added a lot to the fun of the story.<br /><br />Kidnappings – Yes I know but I love them.<br /><br />ALL THE OTHER ALPHA MEN – wowzers Lee Nightingale has a whole stable of bad ass men that I want to get to know better. From the last book I was really interested in Mace but after this one I don’t know whose book I want to read more Vance, Mace or Luke’s. I might be half in love with Luke already.<br /><br /><b>The Story:</b><br /><br />Roxie once upon a time was young and fell in love with the wrong man. She has spent the last year + trying to leave him but he won’t seem to let her go. She has a plan and is in the last stage of it but needs Tex’s help hence the trip to Denver.<br /><br />Hank is a man that knows what he wants when he sees it and the first time he laid eyes on Roxie he knew he wanted her, even if she comes with some baggage. Just because Roxie is a little broken and reluctant doesn’t mean that Hank isn’t going to find a way to get in there.<br /><blockquote>
  <i>“Roxanne, listen closely. One look at you and I knew trouble was on your heels. I’m willin’ to give it time for you to tell me. That doesn’t happen, I’m willin’ to wade in when that trouble catches up. Right now, I’d be doin’ it for Tex and out of curiosity about you. After tonight, I reckon I’ll be doing it for other reasons.”</i>
</blockquote><br />But just as Roxie starts to think maybe she can do this her ex has to show up and ruin everything. Putting Roxie in a lot of danger and making her feel dirty like she doesn’t deserve a good man like Hank and he has a lot more work to do after that.<br /><br />Even though there is an emotional aspect to this love story it is still a lot of fun with chaos at both a strip club and haunted house. The dialogue between characters is fantastic whether it be something funny or sorta serious. Just because you made one mistake in your youth and it took years from your life it doesn’t mean that you are only that choice. You deserve more and sometimes it takes some new friends, a crazy uncle and a badass Alpha to show you how to change your life for the better.<br /><br /><b>A Few Bonuses:</b><br /><br />Seeing the couples from the previous books is always a special treat. I complained that in the last book I didn’t really feel closure on the Jet/Eddie relationship, but seeing them periodically in this you can see they are on the right track and still working on it. Indy and Lee on the other hand and completely there in the relationship department and I love the moments we get with the two of them in this. <br /><br />The building and layering of this series has been a lot of fun and after that last chapter I can’t wait to get into the story of our next couple.</span>
  <a data-text-id="14524627608737000892" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText10483686806756095599" style="display:none"><b>reread:</b> <br>20/05/17<br>15/05/18<br>04/06/19<br><br><i>This is still probably my favourite Rock Chick book. This is full of KA's signature drama, action and angst all wrapped up in one pretty little parcel.<br><br><b>AND HANK HAS AN ADORABLE BROWN LAB NAMED SEAMUS AND I MEAN LOOK AT HIS LTTLE FACE</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1495206508ra/22796334.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I find these books difficult to review because I feel like saying too much more would be ruining the surprise and rush of feelings these books give you. <div id="review_276487839" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/276487839" />
    <a title="Baba  " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4669232-baba"><img alt="Baba  " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1564910043p2/4669232.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/276487839?book_show_action=true">Feb 12, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Baba  " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Baba  " href="/user/show/4669232-baba">Baba  </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer276487839" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5317281482463214980">Hank said to Roxie:<br/><b>"That's what love's all about, Roxanne. You love someone, you trust them always to tell you the truth."<br/><br/>3.5 stars.</b><br/><br/>I enjoyed Rock Chick Redemption, yet it was never as good as RC Revenge, RC Regret or RC Renegade.<br/><br/>Our heroine Roxie is a wild girl. She's finding trouble on a regular basis. Roxie's been on the run from her former boyfriend. Warning: this woman is really high maintenance.<br/><br/><i>I'm going to take a shower. You're going to be good, try not to be sexy or freak me out or anyth</i></span>
  <span id="freeText5317281482463214980" style="display:none">Hank said to Roxie:<br /><b>"That's what love's all about, Roxanne. You love someone, you trust them always to tell you the truth."<br /><br />3.5 stars.</b><br /><br />I enjoyed Rock Chick Redemption, yet it was never as good as RC Revenge, RC Regret or RC Renegade.<br /><br />Our heroine Roxie is a wild girl. She's finding trouble on a regular basis. Roxie's been on the run from her former boyfriend. Warning: this woman is really high maintenance.<br /><br /><i>I'm going to take a shower. You're going to be good, try not to be sexy or freak me out or anything like that. I've got to concentrate, preparing for a formal party is serious business. I don't need distractions."</i><br /><br />But. Did you know that a lot of guys don't like a woman with make-up? <br /><br /><i>"Get dressed. I have to get to work but before that we have to walk Shamus, have breakfast and then you have to spend an hour doing whatever-it-is-you-do that in the end makes you look no more cute and sexy than you do right now."</i><br /><br />Okey dokey, Hank, I think my boyfriend would really like you since he doesn't love make-up either.<br /><br />I think the highlight was the interaction between Roxie and her parents. Boy, it was priceless and Roxie liked to give them a piece of her mind! Trish and Herb were truly hilarious as all get out. Jeez, they were giving lip to each other, and I really loved to see when they were locking horns! Well, Roxie's dad sure knows how to exchange niceties.<br /><br /><i>She can't wear that dress! It's indecent. Her ass is hangin' out."</i> And then he was even so generous to advise Hank by saying: <i>"Son, take my advice, you gotta get this girl in hand. You can't let her run around with her ass hangin' out. You allow it once, she'll do it again. Trust me. I know," Dad told Hank.</i><br /><br />Oh, yeah, and Trish showed her true love when she cared for Hank's house:<br /><br /><i>I looked to Luke (oh, yeah, this badass hot guy was in his element). "Hank's house has been Mom Bombed," I told him.</i><br />Roxie even said…<i>"I've changed my mind, I don't want you to shoot me, I want you to shoot her."</i><br /><br />Let me enlighten you about the Hank kisses. There are the light kisses and the make-you-dizzy kisses. Further, there are the cuddling-with-Hank kisses; they are softer, sweeter, slower, still lots of tongue but mostly just-be-together-and-touch-while-you're-necking kisses. They made Roxie a different kind of dizzy. <i>Oh, yes!</i><br /><br /><br /><b>What didn't work for me:</b><br />Honestly, I didn't love the heroine. She was weepy all the time and her self-doubts of not being worthy of Hank seriously annoyed me. She did it all the time! Yes, please, Roxie you have to explain your Hank-deserves-better-than-you philosophy to me. Maybe I'm a bit slow but I couldn't understand your attitude.<br />I think the book was a bit too long and there were some parts of the plot that dragged a tad too much for me liking.<br /><br />Overall Rock Chick Redemption is a good and fun ride. As long as you don't take this series too seriously and you can overlook quite a few TSTL moments as well as some OTT scenes you will enjoy the Rock Chicks! <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="5317281482463214980" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

        <a title="Kellie Maddox-Ward" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kellie Maddox-Ward" href="/user/show/7309666-kellie-maddox-ward">Kellie Maddox-Ward</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer5318850303225279291">August 2013... <br/><br/>AAGGGHHH I NEED ALLY'S BOOK NOW! I have just spent the past week re-reading all the rock chick books.. I NEED MORE!<br/><br/>May 2012...<br/><b>
  <i>“It looked like GQ was having a convention and all the best looking guys had decided to have a coffee at Fortnum's before going to seminars on how to cope with being really, unbelievably, fucking gorgeous” </i>
</b><br/>YOWZA!<br/><br/><a href='http://media.photobucket.com/image/rock%20chicks/gaarababe/PunkRockChicks.jpg?o=16' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380379176i/735273.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a> How cute is this pic?! Get it.. They're "Rock Chicks."<br/><br/>anyway..<br/><br/>Crazy runs in the family…. <br/><br/>Enter Roxie MacMillan, a HIGH maintenance Rock Ch</span>
  <span id="freeText5318850303225279291" style="display:none">August 2013... <br><br>AAGGGHHH I NEED ALLY'S BOOK NOW! I have just spent the past week re-reading all the rock chick books.. I NEED MORE!<br><br>May 2012...<br><b>
  <i>“It looked like GQ was having a convention and all the best looking guys had decided to have a coffee at Fortnum's before going to seminars on how to cope with being really, unbelievably, fucking gorgeous” </i>
</b><br>YOWZA!<br><br><a href="http://media.photobucket.com/image/rock%20chicks/gaarababe/PunkRockChicks.jpg?o=16" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380379176i/735273.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> How cute is this pic?! Get it.. They're "Rock Chicks."<br><br>anyway..<br><br>Crazy runs in the family…. <br><br>Enter Roxie MacMillan, a HIGH maintenance Rock Chick. She’s also Tex’s niece. <br>The moment she walks into Fortnum’s the whole gang is there and she catches the eye of Hank Nightingale. His “Whisky” eyes know what they want. <br><br>She’s on the run from her ex Billy who won’t believe they are over. She’s been planning a “Sleeping with the Enemy” escape for a while now.<br> Unfortunately he is looking for her and won’t stop. Double unfortunately there are people looking for Billy, so they use her to get to him. <br><br>So here we go again. The whole gang adopts Roxie and then the adventure begins, kidnappings, parties, car chases, etc , new characters are introduced including newcomer Luke (LOVE HIM! And not really new just all clear after the shooting from a few books ago) Roxie’s parents Herb and Trish. Lottie’s opening night as a stripper at Smithies. <br><br>I am seriously in love with these books! They make me LOL, cry <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ well I nearly did when Vance found her in the bathroom and the scenes after that <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> do many many of Luke’s half grin’s!, smile, blush, pull “intense concentration face”, fully grin and LOL some more.<br>The ending was wonderfully written. I actually felt like I was there for the stand off. <br><br>I have serious Lady wood for Luke.. Big time! And Vance, Mace, Darius, even Marcus I love how much he loves Daisy! I’m just loving all these alpha’s and even the non alpha’s/secondary characters, Darius, Smithie, Duke, Tex.. especially Tex he is awesome! <br><br><i>
  <b>What I would like to know is Ally getting her own book?!</b>
</i><br> <br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer705612502" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17784505260118352840"> <b>4,5 “Whisky Stars” !!</b><br/><br/> <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380434617ra/877452.gif' width='400' height='250' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>This third book in this awesome series, tell us the story of Roxie and Hank (Lee’s brother. Remember him? <i>Of course you do!</i> )<br/>For all of you, who just started this series and want to read his story, well: you’ll not be disappointed. <br/><br/>Roxie is Tex’s niece (Crazy coffee master of Fortnum’s) and fell in love only twice in their life. The first time was with Billy, her asshole ex-boyfriend who ruined her to the point the years after she doesn’t feel worthy of anyone. <br/>Much less o</span>
  <span id="freeText17784505260118352840" style="display:none"> <b>4,5 “Whisky Stars” !!</b><br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380434617ra/877452.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This third book in this awesome series, tell us the story of Roxie and Hank (Lee’s brother. Remember him? <i>Of course you do!</i> )<br>For all of you, who just started this series and want to read his story, well: you’ll not be disappointed. <br><br>Roxie is Tex’s niece (Crazy coffee master of Fortnum’s) and fell in love only twice in their life. The first time was with Billy, her asshole ex-boyfriend who ruined her to the point the years after she doesn’t feel worthy of anyone. <br>Much less of the guy who made her fell in love for the second time: Hank. <br>She just wants to run away, forget about the guy who is too good for her and start fresh somewhere else. <br>Yeah, her shithead ex-boyfriend totally deserves a high-five in the face. With a six-hundred pages book. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380434617ra/877453.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>But… oh well, Hank’s having none of it. <br>He knew a lot of women in his life so he knows exactly what he wants and he wants Roxie in his life. And if she has problems, he is there for her even if she doesn’t want him there. (Or think she doesn’t, because everyone around knows that she wants.) <br>So when her, not only asshole but also sick and psychotic, ex-boyfriend comes after her, he is going to be there for her, whatever happens. <br>Even when she tries to run. Using the most sexiest ways to keep her around. <br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380434617ra/877454.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Although the first one is still my favorite, I’m pretty torn between all this guys because I just can’t decide which one of them is my favorite. They are all the most perfect hot bunch of alpha-males ever created. <br>This story is very good and sweeter than the previous ones. And as ever, Kristen Ashley’s heroines are almost as awesome as the heroes. (Almost!) <br>Boy, if you haven’t started these books by now… what the hell are you waiting for? </span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3120498327" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11123842465638735969"><b>3.25 Stars</b><br/><br/><b>Overall Opinion: </b> I realized after a few chapters that I had indeed read this one before, but for some reason, I never wrote a review. I enjoyed parts of it (mainly the crazy side characters) and I liked the h. I just didn't fully feel their connection past lust. I like to experience the development of feelings and I didn't get that here. Yes, there was a lot of craziness and stuff going around them to speed it all up -- but I wasn't feeling the romantic aspects. I'm just not sure I am</span>
  <span id="freeText11123842465638735969" style="display:none"><b>3.25 Stars</b><br /><br /><b>Overall Opinion: </b> I realized after a few chapters that I had indeed read this one before, but for some reason, I never wrote a review. I enjoyed parts of it (mainly the crazy side characters) and I liked the h. I just didn't fully feel their connection past lust. I like to experience the development of feelings and I didn't get that here. Yes, there was a lot of craziness and stuff going around them to speed it all up -- but I wasn't feeling the romantic aspects. I'm just not sure I am a huge fan of the Rock Chick series tbh. I didn't get the amazing ending that I come to expect from KA and I realize that this is probably because we will see what happens with the couple in the later books (like I saw a glimpse of Jet and Eddie's situation), but I would've liked more of a HEA! I didn't hate it, but its not going on my mental list of KA books to re-read either -- a little bit better than 3 "just okay" stars @3.25.<br /><br /><b>Brief Summary of the Storyline: </b> This is Roxi and Hank's story. Roxi is on the run from her ex that doesn't want to be an ex and she heads to Denver where her uncle Tex is. When she goes to the bookstore that Tex works in, she meets Hank. There is an instant and strong connection between the two and Hank instantly starts his strong pursuit of Roxi even though she is warning him off because of her ex drama. There are some suspenseful scenes, some sexy times, some laugh out loud moments...and they get a HFN ending.<br /><br /><b>POV:</b> This was told in Roxi's POV.<br /><br /><b>Overall Pace of Story: </b> Alright. I did skim some but it flowed well for the most part.<br /><br /><b>Instalove:</b>Kind of. The h claims to have "love at first sight" and the H something similar, but I'm not even fully sure I remember them sharing "ILYs" with each other...<br /><br /><b>H rating:</b> 3.5 stars. Hank. I liked him, but I felt like we didn't really get to know him as much as I would've liked. <br /><br /><b>h rating:</b> 4 stars. Roxie. I liked her. She was sassy, strong, vulnerable at the right times, and a little crazy!<br /><br /><b>Sadness level: </b>Low, no tissues needed<br /><br /><b>Push/Pull:</b> Yes <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ The h pushes away a good bit because she doesn't want the H to get hurt. I'd say the H is the main pursuer of the relationship.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Heat level:</b> Good. They have some good tension, chemistry, and scenes -- but not so much it takes away from the story.<br /><br /><b>Descriptive sex:</b> Yes<br /><br /><b>OW/OM drama:</b> Yes <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ The h's ex is after her and causes a bunch of drama <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Sex scene with OW or OM:</b> No<br /><br /><b>Cheating: </b> No<br /><br /><b>Separation:</b> Not really <br /><br /><b>Possible Triggers: </b>Yes <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Violence/kidnapping/murder/criminal activity (on and off page) and mentioned rape of a side character (off page) <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Closure: </b> This ended abruptly with what I would call an HFN ending <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[they are together and going to move in together <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Safety:</b> This one should be <u>Safe with exception</u> for most safety gang readers depending on personal preference<br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<br />- <b>Does Not</b> have cheating<br />- <b>Does Not</b> have a descriptive sex scene with OW/OM<br />- <b> Does</b> have the h pushing the H away<br />- <b> Does Not</b> have a separation between the h and H<br />- <b> Does Not</b> have abuse by mcs<br />- <b>Does Not </b> have a HEA ending <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer6349563948533025193"><u>A Generic Rock Chick review</u><br/><br/><i>[insert name of bad guys]</i> are after <i>[insert name of low life associated with heroine]</i> and because of her association, <i>[insert name of heroine]</i> finds herself a target. All she does is change the names. Being totally honest, <i>Rock Chick Redemption</i> is pretty much exactly </span>
  <span id="freeText6349563948533025193" style="display:none"><u>A Generic Rock Chick review</u><br /><br /><i>[insert name of bad guys]</i> are after <i>[insert name of low life associated with heroine]</i> and because of her association, <i>[insert name of heroine]</i> finds herself a target. Luckily <i>[insert name of alpha hero]</i> has decided she's his girlfriend and will protect her even though she's determined to not get involved with him. <br /><br /><br />I've figured out how KA manages to write so many books. All she does is change the names. Being totally honest, <i>Rock Chick Redemption</i> is pretty much exactly the same book as <i>Rock Chick</i> and <i>Rock Chick Rescue</i>. It was probably 150 pages too long but despite all that it was entertaining enough. I'm going to read the next in the series and I'll probably enjoy it but it's hard to see myself continuing much beyond that.</span>

<div id="review_1057746896" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1057746896" />
    <a title="Choko" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/27962805-choko"><img alt="Choko" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1475642755p2/27962805.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1057746896?book_show_action=true">Sep 17, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Choko" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Choko" href="/user/show/27962805-choko">Choko</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27962805-choko?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1057746896" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13649579665347851806"><b> *** 3.75 *** <br/><br/>A buddy read with the support group for Kristen Ashley Addicts hosted by BBB</b><br/><br/>I have been thinking about not writing reviews for the KA books, because I find myself repeating the same things over and over. KA is a very gifted storyteller who writes Contemporary Romance in a very simple, everyday prose, reaches into the reader's soul, and the unlikely stories with vibrant characters, her Happily ever afters are bitter sweet, always hopefully optimistic, and addictive as chocolate!!! <br/><br/>I</span>
  <span id="freeText13649579665347851806" style="display:none"><b> *** 3.75 *** <br /><br />A buddy read with the support group for Kristen Ashley Addicts hosted by BBB</b><br /><br />I have been thinking about not writing reviews for the KA books, because I find myself repeating the same things over and over. KA is a very gifted storyteller who writes Contemporary Romance in a very simple, everyday prose, reaches into the reader's soul, and the unlikely stories with vibrant characters, her Happily ever afters are bitter sweet, always hopefully optimistic, and addictive as chocolate!!! <br /><br />In this installment we meet Roxy, a mid-western Web designer who is on the run from an ex boyfriend, who is very bad news. She is to visit her uncle, who happens to be our wild and bigger than life friend, Tex!!! Thus she meets all the gang working or hanging out in Indy's café. The gang is as fun and rowdy as always, every member bringing their unique flavor of crazy, mixing and creating a laugh-out- loud entertainment for all of us.<br /><br />The love interest is Hank, a cop, Lee's brother, whisky brown eyes, mind scrambling abs and chest, and as alpha as only KA can make him. Those guys are intimidating even for hot rock Chicks like the high octane, high maintenance, high passion ladies that inhabit KA's imagination. The attraction is instant, the relationship difficult, and the sex always sizzle! But the biggest attraction seems to always be family and friends, and this is what sneaks up on the reader and steals their hearts...<br /><br />I don't want to say much about the plot, since if you are interested, you will find out. I don't want to write a deep dissection of the individual characters. I don't need to speak of the possibility of the plot. The only thing I feel I have to say is that by the power of charm KA infuses in the people, animals and places she writes about, the readers have no choice but come back for more! So, proceed with caution, because these seemingly harmless, unassuming books will get to you too, and soon you will need a support group for Kristen Ashley addiction like me and periodically crave another of her works. And the moment you are ready to admit your addiction, remember that GR has a cozy support group for you in the attic of BBB!!! You are welcome!</span>
  <a data-text-id="13649579665347851806" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/968560947?book_show_action=true">Jun 15, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ingie" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ingie" href="/user/show/15589375-ingie">Ingie</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Audible Audio " href="/book/show/22475277-rock-chick-redemption">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15589375-ingie?shelf=romance-m-f-audio">romance-m-f-audio</a>,
