        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer968560947" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer388610884265970127"><i>Written August 4, 2014</i><br/><br/><b>4.3 "Oh Sweet God" Stars - They just get better and better... I'm now a big fan of these shameless girls and their sexy MEN<br/><br/>Book 3</b><br/><br/>This seems to be a great and more and more loved (audio) book series for me. I liked the first part <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/546672664' rel='nofollow noopener'>#1 - Rock Chick (3.5 stars)</a> about Indy & Lee and even more the second, <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/546673378?book_show_action=false' rel='nofollow noopener'>#2 - Rock Chick Rescue (3.8 stars)</a>, about Jet & Eddie. ~ Will this third book be the best one so far?<br/><br/><b>Yippee, this was great</b>. Do not let go before you've met Hank. ~ What a wonder</span>
  <span id="freeText388610884265970127" style="display:none"><i>Written August 4, 2014</i><br><br><b>4.3 "Oh Sweet God" Stars - They just get better and better... I'm now a big fan of these shameless girls and their sexy MEN<br><br>Book 3</b><br><br>This seems to be a great and more and more loved (audio) book series for me. I liked the first part <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/546672664" rel="nofollow noopener">#1 - Rock Chick (3.5 stars)</a> about Indy &amp; Lee and even more the second, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/546673378?book_show_action=false" rel="nofollow noopener">#2 - Rock Chick Rescue (3.8 stars)</a>, about Jet &amp; Eddie. ~ Will this third book be the best one so far?<br><br><b>Yippee, this was great</b>. Do not let go before you've met Hank. ~ What a wonderful man!! <br><br><a href="http://yoursmiles.org/m-girls.php?page=3" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1403647828ra/10124281.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="http://yoursmiles.org/m-girls.php?page=3" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1403647828ra/10124281.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="http://yoursmiles.org/m-girls.php?page=3" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1403647828ra/10124281.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="http://yoursmiles.org/m-girls.php?page=3" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1403647828ra/10124281.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>It was cozy, enjoyable and some giggly moments to listening to this sweet (quite KA long) love-story.</b><br>14-15 audio hours in this crazy 'chick world' and once more nicely narrated by <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/8109353.Susannah_Jones" title="Susannah Jones" rel="nofollow noopener">Susannah Jones</a>. This third installment felt a tiny bit better than the first and second book. - Even more less "chatter" and more focus on the story topic. Superb fun, hot and very romantic. <br> <br>***********************************************<br><br><i>Rock Chick Redemption</i> (#3) is about <b>Roxie</b> (Roxanne) who is on a run from an old "bad" looser boyfriend (<i>Billy</i>) who just doesn't catch the hint that it is o-v-e-r.<br><blockquote>‘I was done with men. Totally and completely. I was looking forward to a life as a cat lady. I was going to get a dozen cats and a fucking great vibrator, maybe one of those rabbits I heard about, and that was it.’<br><br><a href="http://s1332.photobucket.com/albums/w615/Li64/Hearts/?action=view&amp;current=cf449c656056c8b0afa8d18f3b0f684e_zps77d15586.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1407144934i/10646789.jpg" alt="Photobucket Pictures, Images and Photos" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a>
</blockquote><br><b>It's another wild and funny <i>Rock Chick</i> romance</b> and lovely romantic and hot in the midst of all these screaming crazy friends, kidnappings, car chases, society parties, strip club visits. <br><br>Here are Roxie's amusing uncle <i>Tex</i> and her hilarouis parents, the even crazier small-Indiana-town <i>Herb &amp; Trish</i>. ~ Who doesn't recognize them? I'm just back from a week's big family vacation in a crowded summer-house (!!). <blockquote>“Son, let me tell you something. Even if you don't care, pretend you do. Honestly, it's the best way to go," Dad, the voice of experience, decided to wade in. "She talks about toss pillows. You don't care about toss pillows. You don't even know what toss pillows are. Pretend that toss pillows are your highest priority in life.” </blockquote><br>***********************************************<br><br>...And of course we meet the hottest cop in <i>Denver Colorado</i>, the gorgeous alpha-hunk <b>Hank Nightingale</b> (Lee's brother). The very best <i>RC-Lover</i> so far in my taste. Loved him and every word he said and all the nice stuff he did for Roxie. ~ She <u>so much</u> needed a <u>good</u> man like him.<br><blockquote>
  <a href="http://s1332.photobucket.com/albums/w615/Li64/Couple%20in%20love/?action=view&amp;current=image_zpsb1ee888c.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1407135036i/10645930.jpg" alt="Photobucket Pictures, Images and Photos" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  </a>
</blockquote><br><b>As always, it is a lot of steamy love (well described - never too briefly - never too lengthy)</b> —but a serpentine path to a glorious HEA, some "back &amp; forth" and 'hard' fights. This time I fell hard for the two main characters. Both Roxie and Hank is interesting, exciting and so easy to love. And ...they loved. Yummy nice!!<br><blockquote>‘I pulled out my cell, flipped it opened and said Hank’s name into the phone. It rang twice. <br>“You okay?” he asked in greeting. <br>“My life began when I met you,” I told him. <br>There was a beat of silence. Then, I heard him say, “Sunshine –” </blockquote><br>**********************************************<br><br>I LISTENED, even this third time with this series, on yet a very well-done audiobook. <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/8109353.Susannah_Jones" title="Susannah Jones" rel="nofollow noopener">Susannah Jones</a> does this so good, her narration is just better and better with every book. Her witty and diverse voice, makes it believable and enjoyable at all times. <br><br><b>Higly recommended audiobooks</b> —really affordable reasonably priced, you get a lot for your pennies ($2 or just $6 incl a kindle book). <br><br>**********************************************<br><br><b>It is so good to "be" with all these cool sweet, beautiful and very friendly <i>Denver-Colorado-Rock-Chicks</i></b>.<br>We read about (..and envy them) their nice clothes, sexy sandals, well shaped bodies and long unruly hair. We want to giggles, sighs, groans just like them and WANT to know more about their always so tough and sexy macho men. <br><br><i>Ohmygod,</i> how I like them. Both the chicks, their men and all their friends. They are all irresistible despite all their screaming (or whispering). ~ Ms. Ashley is just an outstanding champion writer on describing these charming, so chaotic and messy, but always compassionate KA worlds.<br><br><b>I LIKE - just plain irresistibly charming</b><br><br><br><br>*******<br><i> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380379176i/735273.jpg" width="80" height="70" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> The <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/series/69392-rock-chick" rel="nofollow noopener">Rock Chick</a> series by <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/2958084.Kristen_Ashley" title="Kristen Ashley" rel="nofollow noopener">Kristen Ashley</a> </i><br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/6538757.Rock_Chick__Rock_Chick___1_" title="Rock Chick (Rock Chick, #1) by Kristen Ashley" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1266750153s/6538757.jpg" alt="Rock Chick (Rock Chick, #1) by Kristen Ashley" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/7405450.Rock_Chick_Rescue__Rock_Chick___2_" title="Rock Chick Rescue (Rock Chick, #2) by Kristen Ashley" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1416398897s/7405450.jpg" alt="Rock Chick Rescue (Rock Chick, #2) by Kristen Ashley" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/9799572.Rock_Chick_Redemption__Rock_Chick___3_" title="Rock Chick Redemption (Rock Chick, #3) by Kristen Ashley" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1409609236s/9799572.jpg" alt="Rock Chick Redemption (Rock Chick, #3) by Kristen Ashley" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a>... and next up: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/10813469.Rock_Chick_Renegade__Rock_Chick___4_" title="Rock Chick Renegade (Rock Chick, #4) by Kristen Ashley" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1328299907s/10813469.jpg" alt="Rock Chick Renegade (Rock Chick, #4) by Kristen Ashley" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a>. </span>
  <a data-text-id="388610884265970127" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mindy Lou&#39;s Book Review" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mindy Lou&#39;s Book Review" href="/user/show/44132489-mindy-lou-s-book-review">Mindy Lou&#39;s Book Review</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Audible Audio " href="/book/show/22475277-rock-chick-redemption">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44132489-mindy-lou-s-book-review?shelf=2018">2018</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2093357715" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8127954235985611286"><i>I’m pretty much repeating my review of book two since it all still applies with a minor adjustment.</i><br/><br/>This is turning out to be a very fun series. I love that the same group of people are in each book. I love that the men are all the gruff, manly men who are dangerous but very protective of their women. The women are outrageously fun, crazy, quirky characters that are keeping the men on their toes. I love their antics and how much trouble they keep getting themselves in. And last but not least, I l</span>
  <span id="freeText8127954235985611286" style="display:none"><i>I’m pretty much repeating my review of book two since it all still applies with a minor adjustment.</i><br /><br />This is turning out to be a very fun series. I love that the same group of people are in each book. I love that the men are all the gruff, manly men who are dangerous but very protective of their women. The women are outrageously fun, crazy, quirky characters that are keeping the men on their toes. I love their antics and how much trouble they keep getting themselves in. And last but not least, I love the side characters who are adding to the overall chaos of the storyline.<br /><br />I know I've already mentioned this but it's worth a second mention...I like that all the men are big hot and very alpha. I love that so far, it's the men chasing the women. Call me old fashioned but I want to see the man go after the woman. I even like that the women are resisting BUT I do wish it was toned down a bit. I enjoy some resistance by the heroine but throughout most of the book. <br /><br />I'm looking forward to the next crazy adventure in book 4. Oh and I'm listening to the audio books and the narrator is fantastic! She is adding so much to the books with her interpretation. I highly recommend the audiobooks!</span>
  <a data-text-id="8127954235985611286" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

It's great as well having all the Rock Chick & Hot Guys coming along for the ride. <br/><br/>I found this story to be emotional at times and it made me laugh out loud and I could not put it down I had to know what was going to happen next for Roxie and Hank.<br/><br/>Moving on to Vance now :-)<br/><br/><b>After reading the eight books in the Rock Chick series and meeting every rock chick and hot</b></span>

<div id="review_263365096" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/263365096" />
    <a title="Duchess Nicole" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2204947-duchess-nicole"><img alt="Duchess Nicole" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1499265843p2/2204947.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/263365096?book_show_action=true">Jan 17, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Duchess Nicole" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Duchess Nicole" href="/user/show/2204947-duchess-nicole">Duchess Nicole</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=genre-romantic-suspense">genre-romantic-suspense</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=genre-contemp-romance">genre-contemp-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=read-in-2012">read-in-2012</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=e-pcs">e-pcs</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer263365096" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15002777731147608799">"I'm going to take a shower. You're going to be good, try not to be sexy or freak me out or anything like that. I've got to concentrate, preparing for a formal party is serious business. I don't need distractions." <br/><br/>And what's hilarious about that, other than the obvious, is that she wasn't talking to our hero, Hank, but another of the 'boy brigade.' Holy effing hotness. KA does it again. Each time I think that I find something wrong with one of these books, there's that giddy feeling that I get </span>
  <span id="freeText15002777731147608799" style="display:none">"I'm going to take a shower. You're going to be good, try not to be sexy or freak me out or anything like that. I've got to concentrate, preparing for a formal party is serious business. I don't need distractions." <br /><br />And what's hilarious about that, other than the obvious, is that she wasn't talking to our hero, Hank, but another of the 'boy brigade.' Holy effing hotness. KA does it again. Each time I think that I find something wrong with one of these books, there's that giddy feeling that I get and a voice in the back of my head that says "WHO FREAKIN' CARES?" <br /><br />Example: Every single one of the first three Rock Chicks have had one of the other super hot bad boys give them the half-lidded, sleepy eyed sexy stare and begin to fall in love with them. It serves no other purpose but to freak them out and make their hoo ha tingle. Like my mind says sometimes, "WHO FREAKIN' CARES"? It's a good enough situation to use over and over again. These women have insecurities. Well, hell, just bring them over to the Rock Chicks and let the boys have a go at them. A few tender touches, tons of sexy stares and dizzying moments, and BAM! Even I feel hot, and I'm just reading. <br /><br />Hank is the first in the Rock Chick to feel a bit insecure himself, and it fit perfectly. It was enough to change up the story just a bit and hold off a <i>tiny</i> bit of the confidence that seems to roll off these men in huge, crashing waves. He's the good guy, the boy next door cop who finally decides that there are some shades of gray in life, and he's not afraid to finally explore them when his woman is threatened.<br /><br />Roxanne is a high maintenance Rock Chick running from her past. Her long lost uncle is none other than TEX! Which lends quite a bit of hilarity to the situation. When Roxy (and isn't that a rock chick name?!) runs into Hank, it truly is love at first sight. But she's got the feeling that she's just not good enough for him. When her past follows her to Denver, its a darn good thing she's got the Nightingale boys behind her.<br /><br />Aside from the other secondary characters that I already love, a few more are introduced. This one is just as lively as the first two, and the action starts even sooner. Great read! I'm blowing through these too fast to be believed. <br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="15002777731147608799" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_578067019" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/578067019" />
    <a title="Michelle" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13126896-michelle"><img alt="Michelle" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1505605297p2/13126896.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/578067019?book_show_action=true">Jan 03, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Michelle" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Michelle" href="/user/show/13126896-michelle">Michelle</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/11061690-rock-chick-redemption">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer578067019" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10676113843045461815">Rock Chick Redemption is the story of Roxie and Hank. Can I just say that Hank was all sorts of swoony? And Luke? OMG. He gave me tingles. Although I did get a bit squirmy over the affection these badasses keep showing their friend’s women. <br/><br/><br/>Roxie is gearing up to make the break from the bad news of her past and devises a plan that leads her to Denver and in the arms of her Uncle Tex, only her plan is shit and before she can say no, the whole gang has decided to take up her cause. Including Hank.</span>
  <span id="freeText10676113843045461815" style="display:none">Rock Chick Redemption is the story of Roxie and Hank. Can I just say that Hank was all sorts of swoony? And Luke? OMG. He gave me tingles. Although I did get a bit squirmy over the affection these badasses keep showing their friend’s women. <br /><br /><br />Roxie is gearing up to make the break from the bad news of her past and devises a plan that leads her to Denver and in the arms of her Uncle Tex, only her plan is shit and before she can say no, the whole gang has decided to take up her cause. Including Hank. <br /><br />Especially Hank.<br /><br />But with a bit of dirt left on her from her slime ball ex, Roxie isn’t sure someone as good as Hank should end up with the likes of her. Only Hank doesn’t quite agree and decides to show her this by laying it all hang out and not letting herself talk or think her way out of it.<br /><br />When her ex comes for her before she can get her plan fully in order, it sets of a chain reaction where all the Rock Chicks and their men are called in for the rescue. <br /><br />The story of Hank and Roxie is just as action packed as the prior stories, but it was a bit softer. There was just something about Hank that made me feel like he was just waiting for his woman to show up. Not that he was just smart enough to grab a good one once he saw one. Like he was sort of longing for that bit of sweet in his life. Needing it to combat and erase the ugly he had to see with his job.<br /><br />And although Roxie took some convincing. I loved that she wasn’t too stubborn in that annoying way. And as much as I hate that I took so long to jump into this series, I am sort of happy that I waited and get to enjoy it now. I am looking forward to Vance’s story – but really am trying hard not to jump straight to Luke’s.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="10676113843045461815" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1100046607" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7720807892586525596">I can't get enough of this series. Seriously. Another amazing read. <b>Exciting, entertaining, and sexy. Loved it!</b><br/><br/>I loved Hank and Roxie's story. It was chalked full of Rock Chick goodness. Hank is just so adorable and good and loving and even though he's got the sexy alpha male thing going on, he's is a bit softer but more sweet than commanding. I thought Roxie was a great character and so different than the other girls but she did have that awesome attitude. She seemed so much more vulnerable and</span>
  <span id="freeText7720807892586525596" style="display:none">I can't get enough of this series. Seriously. Another amazing read. <b>Exciting, entertaining, and sexy. Loved it!</b><br /><br />I loved Hank and Roxie's story. It was chalked full of Rock Chick goodness. Hank is just so adorable and good and loving and even though he's got the sexy alpha male thing going on, he's is a bit softer but more sweet than commanding. I thought Roxie was a great character and so different than the other girls but she did have that awesome attitude. She seemed so much more vulnerable and and very relatable to me. I loved how she didn't go seeking out trouble. <br /><br />Hank and Roxie had a sweet and entertaining relationship. I adore the nickname she gave him. Loved their hot times and Hank’s sexy ways. He might be my new favorite Rock Chick man to date. <br /><br />This was full of drama and adventure and I loved the pacing and how it played out. In between there where lighters moments and they made laugh out loud. Roxie's parents provided so much entertainment, I was literally laughing so hard I had tears in my eyes. They were priceless! <br /><br />There was more of all the guys and their women and I think it's just a great cast of characters. These books can be read as stand alone but I'm glad I'm reading on order because knowing the back stories make some things even funnier. All the men are so sexy with distinct personalities, I cannot wait Vance, Mace and Luke's stories. The end of this pulls you into the next book, <i>Rock Chick Renegade</i> (it’s time for Vance, yeah!!!). <br /><br /><b>Excellent story with great characters and lots attention to detail. Kristen Ashley is officially a favorite. #rockchickforever.</b></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer10729145621242319714"><b>4.5 Whiskey STARS</b><br/><br/>I'm having a blast with these Rock Chicks. This was Hank Nightingale's story. I'll admit, I thought Hank might be too goody two shoes because he was a cop. But damn, KA gave me another sexy, commanding and dominant hero! I'm having a hard time picking my fave Alpha from this series.<br/><br/>And hot damn, I FINALLY met Luke! KA had mentioned him several times in the other two books and I was anxious to meet him. Boy oh boy, he was so worth the wait.<br/><br/><a href='http://imgur.com/eRtHDlV' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1468714233ra/19739535.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>

</a><br><br>Man, I need more Luke *sigh*<br><br>I also really like Roxie and enjoyed the entire Rock Chick gang! This had the perfect mix of angst, sweet and sexy. <br><br>**Audiobook**</span>

<div id="review_280350681" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/280350681" />
    <a title="~ Becs ~" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2626261-becs"><img alt="~ Becs ~" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1388693144p2/2626261.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/280350681?book_show_action=true">Feb 19, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="~ Becs ~" class="user" itemprop="url" name="~ Becs ~" href="/user/show/2626261-becs">~ Becs ~</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=kindle">kindle</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=alpha-hero">alpha-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=abused-heroine">abused-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=cop-hero">cop-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=romantic-suspense">romantic-suspense</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer280350681" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7227486780140943966">Well this is book 3 in the Rock Chick series and starts up about 48 hours after <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/7405450.Rock_Chick_Rescue__Rock_Chick___2_' title='Rock Chick Rescue (Rock Chick, #2) by Kristen Ashley' rel='nofollow noopener'>Rock Chick Rescue</a> left off.<br/><br/>Roxie has been running from a bad relationship with Billy. She's been with him for years and considered herself in love with him. He filled her full of hope and promise but the promises turned out to be largely false and she has been trying to leave him for years. Every time she runs, he finds her and takes her back. Now Roxie has run to Denver, more specifically to Fortnums, to find good o</span>
  <span id="freeText7227486780140943966" style="display:none">Well this is book 3 in the Rock Chick series and starts up about 48 hours after <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/7405450.Rock_Chick_Rescue__Rock_Chick___2_" title="Rock Chick Rescue (Rock Chick, #2) by Kristen Ashley" rel="nofollow noopener">Rock Chick Rescue</a> left off.<br /><br />Roxie has been running from a bad relationship with Billy. She's been with him for years and considered herself in love with him. He filled her full of hope and promise but the promises turned out to be largely false and she has been trying to leave him for years. Every time she runs, he finds her and takes her back. Now Roxie has run to Denver, more specifically to Fortnums, to find good ole Uncle Tex (who, incidentally, is my most favourite secondary character in a series ever). <br /><br />As she walks into Fortnums, the Hot Crew are lazing on the sofas and she takes one look at Hank and it is love at first sight. He spots her and feels the same way and the very next day, they are on their first date. It's deeply romantic with horse-drawn carriages and tears and they spend the night together. The next morning we have this scene..............<br /><br /><i>“Tell me one thing, are you in danger?”<br />I lost my scowl and felt my body begin to melt.<br />Shit.<br />He was worried about me.<br />Billy had taken a sledgehammer to the door and he’d put his arm to my throat, once. Even after years of me running away and more than a year of no sex, he’d never raised a hand to me after the arm incident. He was intense, that was for certain, but every time I pretended to escape, he brought me back by talking me into it (or, at least, I let him think that). <br />I didn’t think I was in danger. I was just trapped. <br />“I’m not in danger, I just have… a situation. I’m fixing it,” I told Hank.</i><br /><br />Hank believes her and takes his dog out for a walk but Roxie <i>is</i> in danger and the story roars into life from this moment on and you'll need to hold on because it's another Kristen Ashley roller-coaster breathtaking ride.<br /><br />Of course, Roxie doesn't consider herself good enough for Hank. She's sees him as a straight arrow, a cop who only sees in black and white, right and wrong and she considers herself tainted by her association with Billy who was into some serious bad business that Roxie was in complete ignorance of. Hank calls her on this constantly and just won't let her get away with it.<br /><br />Funniest moment of the book - Hank getting Mombombed!!!<br /><br />We have all the usual crew in attendance. Lee and Indy with Indy, as usual, getting into trouble. Eddie and Jet still arguing but mostly loved up. Ally and Carl, still dating. The mysterious Jane still wafting around the aisles of the bookstore. Tod and Stevie outrageously trying to plan a totally OTT colour scheme for Lee and Indy's wedding. Daisy and Shirleen, larger than life and of course Tex, who is still seeing Jet's Mom, and we learn a bit more about him in this story.<br /><br />The Hot Crew are all there, mostly Vance and Luke, who has recovered from being shot way back in book 1. I fell a little bit in love with Luke during this one and can't wait for his book.<br /><br />It's another great romantic suspense story from Kristen Ashely and I've been trying to pinpoint exactly what it is that I love about her books. All the scenes come vividly to mind and the characters seem so real, they almost jump off the pages and I think this is tantamount to the descriptive writing. She sure knows how to set a scene. The plots are far-fetched, the heroes wonderful but unreal but I think it all boils down to the fact that she just has a natural God given talent at story telling and I am enjoying every second.<br /><br />4 stars - romantic suspense.<br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="7227486780140943966" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('Al6X0jePkjPsuxEoSgaYc59J2gH7MPGXeQzySnLlL5JeH50l2jSrsKA6RRvY7Q7xgwnAZoPfdbppehbGZBZreQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('HK9RugJ10q+g7n0inVwr8rv49mDj3H3LLY9v+AUXBWhA7ltN787rLOxvKREPt71wp7jsB5sz+eY9+Yt0E+RBgw==')})
  }

  <span id="freeText17183892705533010013" style="display:none">Kristen Ashley was born in Gary, Indiana, USA. She nearly killed her mother and herself making it into the world, seeing as she had the umbilical cord wrapped around her neck (already attempting to accessorise and she hadn't taken her first breath!). <br /><br />Kristen grew up in Brownsburg, Indiana but has lived in Denver, Colorado and the West Country of England. Thus she has been blessed to have friends and family around the globe. Her posse is loopy (to say the least) but loopy is good when you want to write.<br /><br />Kristen was raised in a house with a large and multi-generational family. They lived on a very small farm in a small town in the heartland and existed amongst the strains of Glenn Miller, The Everly Brothers, REO Speedwagon and Whitesnake (and the wardrobes that matched).<br /><br />Needless to say, growing up in a house full of music, clothes and love was a good way to grow up. <br /><br />And as she keeps growing up, it keeps getting better.</span>
